 Lingayats do not worship the Lord Shiva of the Hindus but provide a way to worship the Lord in the proper shape as "ishtalinga"

 lingayat main shavon ko dafnaaya jaataa he

 usee kii galat nitiyon ke kaaran pradesh main garibi va berogari badi or log duusare rajyon main palaayan ke liye majaboor hue
 " congress mahasachiv rahul gandhi or prachaar karne amethi pahunchin unki bahan priyanka gandhi par nishaanaa sadhate hue mayawati ne kaha, "donon bhai-bahanon ke paas alladin kaa chiraag he, jo paanch saal main rajya kii tasviir badalane kii baat karte hai
 Priyanka's concern about the development of Uttar Pradesh is useless, which is never seen and goes only to seek votes at the time of elections
 " Mayawati said, "when the Congress could not develop the state after being in power for forty years, how will its crown prince (rahul Gandhi) do it in five years
 " unhone kaha ki raibareli or amethi jahaan se congress ke saansad or vidhayak jitate hai, vahaan bhi congress ne koi vikaas nahin kiya
 Continuing the attack on the Congress party in the election campaign, Mayawati said, "if Congress, which committed 62 scams in 31 months, came to power in Uttar Pradesh, unemployment and poverty would again increase
 "tippaniyan Accusing the Congress-led central government of discrimination, Mayawati said, "our demand for a package of thousands of rupees for the overall development of Uttar Pradesh is not accepted by the Congress
 " Mayawati said that if the Samajwadi Party (SP) came to power, the goons would run the police station and the respect of the daughters-in-law would not be safe and if the Bharatiya Janata Party (BJP) came to power, communalism would increase so much that it would be difficult to live
 purvachal ke maharajaganj main chunavi jansabha ko sambodhit karte hue mayawati ne kaha, "uttar pradesh main sabase zyada samay 40 saal tak congress ne raaj kiya
 Due to his wrong policies, poverty and unemployment increased in the state and people were forced to migrate to other states
 " Hitting out at Congress general secretary Rahul Gandhi and his sister Priyanka Gandhi, who reached Amethi to campaign, Mayawati said, "both siblings have Aladdin's lamp, which talks of changing the state's picture in five years
 uttar pradesh ke vikaas ko lekar priyanka kii chintaa bekaar he, jo kabhi najar nahin aatin or keval chunaav ke samay vot maangane ke liye chali aati hai
 " mayawati ne kaha, "jab chalis saal tak satta main rahane par congress pradesh kaa vikaas nahin kar pai to uske yuvaraj (rahul gandhi) paanch saal main kaise karenge
 "he said that from where Rae Bareli and Amethi win Congress mps and mlas, the Congress did not make any development there
 chunaav prachaar abhiyaan main congress party par hamalaa jari rakhte hue mayawati ne kaha, "31 maheene ke kaarykaal main 62 ghotaale karne vaali congress agar uttar pradesh kii satta main aa gai to phir se berogari or garibi bad jaaegi
 "comments congress-nit centre sarkaar par bhedbhaav kaa aarope lagaate hue mayawati ne kaha, "uttar pradesh ke samgr vikaas ke liye hajaaron rupee ke package kii hamaari maang congress ne sweekaar nahin kii
 " mayawati ne kaha ki agar samaajawaadee party (sapa) satta main aa gai to gunde thane chalaayenge or bahu-betiyon kii izzat mahfuj nahin rahegi or agar bhartiya janata party (bhaajapa) satta main aa gai to sampradayikta itani bad jaaegi ki rahanaa mushkil ho jayega

 At the end of this month, on September 30, when the BCCI selectors sit down to select teams for one-day and T20 against Australia, they will have to sort the talent from the middle order
 chayankarta virendra sahvaag ko middle order main kaise feet kar paaenge yah bahut bada sawaal he
 According to a statement by former Australian captain Ian Chappell, Sehwag has offered to land himself in the middle order, but neither will the team benefit him nor Sehwag himself
 australia ke khilaaf team india kaa chunaav karte vakt chayankartaaon kii ulajhanein badi hui hongi, kyonki khabaron ke mutabik virendra sahvaag ne middle order main khilne kii na sirf peshkash kii he, balki chalanger cap main tej ardhshtkeey pari khel apni daavedaari majboot bhi kar di he
 In the Challenger Trophy tournament, Virender Sehwag landed in the middle order after many years, at number four
 india blue ke khilaaf dilli ke liye khelte hue viru kaa andaaz zaraa bhi nahin badla
 It is also important for Sehwag and his fans that Chief Selector Sandeep Patil was witness to this atishi innings
 38 gendon par 59 ran kii pari main sahvaag ne nau chauke or ek chakka laga kar sanket diya ki na to unke balle main jang laga he na andaaz badla he
 But in spite of all this, while selecting Team India on September 30, will the selectors give Sehwag a place in the middle order
 sahvaag ne lambey samay ke baad middle order main ballebaazi main khud ko aazamaane kaa faisalaa kiya he, lekin khud sahvaag kaa record Do not see with them
 sahvaag ne 251 van-de match khele hai, jinamein unhone 35
 Has scored 8273 runs at an average of 05
 isamen unki 15 shatkeey paariyaan bhi shaamil hai, lekin middle order main unhone sirf 37 van-de match khele hai, jinamein unhone 25
 Has scored 755 runs at an average of 16
 is dauraan unhone sirf ek shatak lagaaya
 In such a situation, Sehwag can be included in the team in place of Suresh Raina and Dinesh Karthik in the middle order
 haalanki, dinesh karthik kaa balla pichley maheenon main india−e kii ore se khelte hue kuch khaas nahin chalaa, lekin dinesh karthik ne champions trophy ke dauraan paanch maichon main 41 ke ausat se 82 ran banaae
 While Suresh Raina played many important innings while playing for india-a, Suresh Raina scored 8 in five matches during the Champions Trophy
 50 ke ausat se sirf 17 ran banaae

 chalanger trophy toornament main virendra sahvaag kai saal baad middle order main utre, chauthe number par

 sahvaag or unke phans ke liye ahm yah bhi he ki mukhya chayankarta sandip patil is aatishi pari ke gavaah rahe
 In his 59-run knock off 38 balls, Sehwag hit nine fours and a six to indicate that neither his bat was rusted nor had his style changed
 lekin, in sabake baavjood 30 sitambar ko team india kaa chayan karte vakt kya chayankarta sahvaag ko middle order main jagah denge
 Sehwag has decided to try himself in batting in the middle order after a long time, but Sehwag's own record unke saath nahin dikh rahaa
 Sehwag has played 251 one-day matches, of which he has 35
 05 kii ausat se 8273 ran banaae hai
 This includes his 15 century innings, but in the middle order he has played only 37 one-day matches, of which he has 25
 16 ke ausat se 755 ran banaae hai
 During this he scored just one century
 aise main sahvaag ko middle order main suresh raina, dinesh karthik kii jagah team main shaamil kiye ja sakate hai
 Although Dinesh Karthik's bat did not fare much in the last months playing for india-a, Dinesh Karthik scored 82 runs in five matches at an average of 41 during the Champions Trophy
 jabaki suresh raina ne india−e kii ore se khelte hue kai ahm paariyaan khelin, lekin champions trophy ke dauraan suresh raina ne paanch maichon main 8
 Scored just 17 runs at an average of 50
 tippaniyan In the middle order, Yuvraj Singh is also presenting his strong claim
 india−e ke captain ke taur par isi maheene shatak or ardhshtak laga kar unhone chayankarton ko thos sandesh de diya he

 In the instant messaging app whatsapp, after the video calling feature, a new security based feature has now come
 yah tu factor othentication he jo jimail bhi diya jaataa he
 According to reports, this new version has been given in the beta app and currently it has been seen in Windows Phone
 ise actevet karne ke baad yugers se chah disit kaa pascode maanga jayega jo unke registerd mobile par bheja jayega
 Although this may seem troublesome to many people, it is difficult for them to pass the bar passcode
 lekin jo log zyada security chaahate hai unke liye yah feechar behtareen sabit hoga
 After this, Criminals also make a clone of your smartphone, then they can not use your whatsapp
 philhal yah feechar beta varjan main he, lekin agar aapako bhi chahie to aap ise apike mirar se downlod kar sakate hai or beta tester ke liye rogistor kara sakate hai
 It seems like whatsapp has made it optional, ie if you want to use it or not
 iske liye aapako whatsap kii settings menjakar acount par clikkarna he
 Here you will see the option of two stay verification
 yahaan clic karke aap ise actevet kar sakate hai
 Apart from the background audio feature to step verification, a new feature has been added to the beta version of the whatsapp app for Android
 iske tahat ab audio massej ko whatsap ke becoground main chalaa sakate hai
 a report from the tech website Android Police, whatsapp can now play whatsapp audio messages while using other apps
